/Docker/config/extract_words.sh:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
1 | #! /bin/bash
2 | 
3 | grep --include='*.py' --include='*.html' --include='*.txt' -Roh -e 'word(u*"[^"]*"[,)]' -e "word(u*'[^']*'[,)]" | sed -e 's/word(u*"\(.*\)"[,)]/"\1": Null/' -e "s/word(u*'\(.*\)'[,)]/\"\1\": Null/" | sort | uniq
4 |

/Docker/process-email.sh:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 1 | #!/bin/bash
 2 | 
 3 | export DA_ROOT="${DA_ROOT:-/usr/share/docassemble}"
 4 | export DA_DEFAULT_LOCAL="local3.10"
 5 | 
 6 | export DA_ACTIVATE="${DA_PYTHON:-${DA_ROOT}/${DA_DEFAULT_LOCAL}}/bin/activate"
 7 | source "${DA_ACTIVATE}"
 8 | 
 9 | emailfile="$(mktemp)"
10 | 
11 | cat > "$emailfile"
12 | python -m docassemble.webapp.process_email "$emailfile"
13 | rm -f "$emailfile"
14 |

/Docker/restart-nginx.sh:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 1 | #! /bin/bash
 2 | 
 3 | if [ "${DASUPERVISORUSERNAME:-null}" != "null" ]; then
 4 |     SUPERVISORCMD="supervisorctl --serverurl http://localhost:9001 --username ${DASUPERVISORUSERNAME} --password ${DASUPERVISORPASSWORD}"
 5 | else
 6 |     SUPERVISORCMD="supervisorctl --serverurl http://localhost:9001"
 7 | fi
 8 | 
 9 | ${SUPERVISORCMD} restart nginx > /dev/null
10 |
